<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:аванс.html>ава́нс</a> (10265)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">avance</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аванс.html>ава́нс</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aváns</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аванс.html>ава́нса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аванс.html>ава́нсы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:аванс.html>ава́нсов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>advance <i>(of money)</i>, prepayment, payment on account</li>
<li><i>(plural, figurative)</i> advances, overtures</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:авантюра.html>авантю́ра</a> (10916)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">aventure</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">adventura</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">advenire</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to come</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюра.html>авантю́ра</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avantjúra</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюра.html>авантю́ры</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюра.html>авантю́ры</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюра.html>авантю́р</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюрный.html>авантю́рный</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> adventure, venture</li></ol>

</p>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a><span class="hyph-dot" style="color:red;">·</span>ван<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>тю<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ст</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:одушевленный.html>одушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:мужской.html>мужско́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 2-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 1a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюра.html>авантю́ра</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avantjúra</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авантюрный.html>авантю́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avantjúrnyj</span>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a> (5534)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Italian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Italian language">Italian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="it">avaria</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">عَوَارِيَّة</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʿawāriyya</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">damaged goods</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">عَوَار</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʿawār</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fault, blemish, defect, flaw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">عَوِرَ</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ʿawira</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to lose an eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avárija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>damage, breakdown, fault, failure, crash (<i>rarely</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скважина.html>сква́жине</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> v skvážine</i> ― <span class="e-translation">downhole failure</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:двигатель.html>дви́гателя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> dvígatelja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">engine failure</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́мы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> sistémy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">system fault</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:система.html>систе́мы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> vsej sistémy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">blackout</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>accident, crash, wreck, emergency, average (<i>i.e. situation caused by damage, breakdown or failure</i>).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дна</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> súdna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shipwreck</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чае</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рии</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v slúčaje <b>avárii</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in case of an emergency</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чае</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рии</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдернуть.html>вы́дернуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шнур.html>шнур</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:выдавить.html>вы́давить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стекло.html>стекло́</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">typical emergency guide in Russian buses</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v slúčaje <b>avárii</b> výdernutʹ šnur, výdavitʹ stekló</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">in case of an emergency pull out the cord and push out the pane</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морской.html>морска́я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">morskája <b>avárija</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">accident at sea</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:потерпеть.html>потерпе́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рию</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">poterpétʹ <b>aváriju</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crash, to have an accident</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> полёте</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> v poljóte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in-flight accident</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:энергосистема.html>энергосисте́ме</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> v enɛrgosistéme</i> ― <span class="e-translation">power interruption</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рия</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:судно.html>су́дне</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>avárija</b> na súdne</i> ― <span class="e-translation">average on a vessel</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:много.html>мно́го</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авария.html>ава́рий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́гах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mnógo <b>avárij</b> na dorógax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">many road-related <b>accidents</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> misfortune</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгуст</a> (1639)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">авъгустъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avŭgustŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Αὔγουστος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Aúgoustos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">Augustus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгуст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ávgust</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгуста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгусты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгустов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>August
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгусте</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ávguste</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">in August</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:август.html>а́вгусте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́да</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>ávguste</b> étovo góda</i> ― <span class="e-translation">in August</span></div></dd>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:августейший.html>августе́йший</a> (29272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">augustus</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́йший</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-éjšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; formally a superlative.
</p>

</p>

***авианосец.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:авианосец.html>авиано́сец</a> (32031)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>First attested in 1927. From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">авиа-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avia-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:носить.html>носи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nosítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ец</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, an inexact calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Flugzeugträger</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:авиационный.html>авиацио́нный</a> (6049)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авиация.html>авиа́ция</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aviácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авиационный.html>авиацио́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">aviaciónnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> aviation, aircraft

***авось.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a> (9176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́се</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">avose</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">a</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">but</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:оса.html>осе́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">OseEtymology_1</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">here</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avósʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> perhaps, maybe, possibly, may still, might yet <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">low certainty</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:повезти.html>повезёт</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Avósʹ</b> povezjót.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">We/I may yet succeed. (with low certainty)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avósʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́ся</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́си</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blind trust in divine providence; blind faith in sheer luck; blind trust in sheer luck; counting on a miracle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:надеяться.html>наде́ясь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:решить.html>реши́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выехать.html>вы́ехать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:встречный.html>встре́чную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:полоса.html>по́лосу</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чтобы.html>что́бы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:объехать.html>объе́хать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пробка.html>про́бку</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nadéjasʹ na <b>avósʹ</b>, ja rešíl výjexatʹ na vstréčnuju pólosu, štóby obʺjéxatʹ próbku.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Counting on a <b>miracle</b>, I decided to slip into the oncoming lane to get around the traffic jam.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>faith in serendipity; counting on pure luck
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:русский.html>ру́сский</a> «<b><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></b>»</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">rússkij “<b>avósʹ</b>”</i> ― <span class="e-translation">said about the alleged unconcern of Russians and their tendency to rely on luck</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>avósʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">counting on pure luck</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> небо́сем <a href = vnd.unilang:водиться.html>води́лись</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оба.html>о́ба</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яма.html>я́му</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ввалиться.html>ввали́лись</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Avósʹ</b> s nebósem vodílisʹ, da óba v jámu vvalílisʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"Avos" and "Nebos" hung out together and both fell into a hole. (one can't rely on luck alone)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>От́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авось.html>аво́ся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:добрый.html>добра́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>жди́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ot <b>avósja</b> dobrá ne ždi.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't expect anything good from "Avos". (one can't rely on luck alone)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авоська.html>аво́ська</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avósʹka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авоська.html>аво́ськи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авоська.html>аво́ськи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авоська.html>аво́сек</a></b>)

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Auto</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:авто.html>авто́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avtó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>indeclinable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> car, wheels
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:полюбоваться.html>полюбу́йтесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:новый.html>но́вое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:авто.html>авто́</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Poljubújtesʹ na mojó nóvoje <b>avtó</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Behold my new car!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бус</a> (1371)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_5">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Probably borrowed  from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">autobus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Autobus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">autobus</i> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">autobus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бус</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">avtóbus</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́буса</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бусы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бусов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>bus, motorbus
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́лись</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:автобус.html>авто́бус</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vídel, kak oní sadílisʹ v <b>avtóbus</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I saw them getting on the bus.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b>ав<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ма<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:ти.html>ти</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:зи.html>зи́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ро<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ван<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
